Introduction

Base URL: http://localhost:8002

This documentation aims to provide all the information you need to work with our API.

As you scroll, you'll see code examples for working with the API in different programming languages in the dark area to the right (or as part of the content on mobile). You can switch the language used with the tabs at the top right (or from the nav menu at the top left on mobile).

Authenticating requests

This API is not authenticated.

Endpoints

GET api/user

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://localhost:8002/api/user" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8002/api/user"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());

Example response (401):

Show headers 
cache-control: no-cache, private
content-type: application/json
access-control-allow-origin: *
 

{
    "message": "Unauthenticated."
}
Received response:
Request failed with error:


Tip: Check that you're properly connected to the network.
If you're a maintainer of ths API, verify that your API is running and you've enabled CORS.
You can check the Dev Tools console for debugging information.

Request      

GET api/user

Headers

Accept      

Example: application/json

GET api/get-all-categories

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://localhost:8002/api/get-all-categories" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8002/api/get-all-categories"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());

With their efficient cooling capabilities and affordability, air coolers provide a viable alternative to air conditioners. In this article, we will explore the various aspects of air coolers in Nepal, including their types, factors to consider when buying, popular brands, price ranges, and the best options available in the market.</span></p><p><br></p><h2><span class=\"ql-size-large\">Introduction</span></h2><p><br></p><p><span class=\"ql-size-large\">Air coolers, also known as evaporative coolers, are devices that use the natural process of evaporation to cool the air. They work by drawing in warm air from the surroundings, passing it through a cooling pad saturated with water, and then blowing out cool air. This process creates a refreshing and comfortable environment, making air coolers popular among households in Nepal.</span></p><h2><br></h2><h2><span class=\"ql-size-large\">Types of Air Coolers</span></h2><p><br></p><p><span class=\"ql-size-large\">There are several types of air coolers available in the market, each catering to different needs and preferences.</span></p><p><br></p><p><span class=\"ql-size-large\">Desert Coolers</span></p><p><br></p><p><span class=\"ql-size-large\">Desert coolers are large-capacity air coolers suitable for cooling larger spaces like living rooms or offices. They have a higher cooling capacity and a larger water tank capacity, allowing them to provide effective cooling for extended periods.</span></p><p><br></p><p><span class=\"ql-size-large\">Personal Air Coolers</span></p><p><br></p><p><span class=\"ql-size-large\">Personal air coolers, also known as room coolers, are compact and portable. They are designed to cool smaller areas such as bedrooms or study rooms. These coolers are ideal for individual use and are more energy-efficient compared to desert coolers.</span></p><p><br></p><p><span class=\"ql-size-large\">Tower Air Coolers</span></p><p><br></p><p><span class=\"ql-size-large\">Tower air coolers are tall and sleek, designed to fit in narrow spaces. They provide powerful and efficient cooling while occupying minimal floor space. Tower coolers are suitable for both small and medium-sized rooms.</span></p><p><br></p><p><span class=\"ql-size-large\">Factors to Consider When Buying an Air Cooler</span></p><p><br></p><p><span class=\"ql-size-large\">When purchasing an air cooler in Nepal, several factors should be taken into consideration to ensure you make the right choice.</span></p><p><br></p><p><span class=\"ql-size-large\">Cooling Capacity</span></p><p><br></p><p><span class=\"ql-size-large\">The cooling capacity of an air cooler determines its effectiveness in cooling a given area. It is measured in cubic meters per hour (m³/h). Consider the size of the room or space you intend to cool and choose an air cooler with an appropriate cooling capacity.</span></p><p><br></p><p><span class=\"ql-size-large\">Water Tank Capacity</span></p><p><br></p><p><span class=\"ql-size-large\">The water tank capacity determines the duration for which the air cooler can provide continuous cooling without refilling. Larger water tanks are suitable for longer cooling periods, while smaller tanks may require frequent refilling.</span></p><p><br></p><p><span class=\"ql-size-large\">Energy Efficiency</span></p><p><br></p><p><span class=\"ql-size-large\">Look for air coolers with energy-efficient features to minimize electricity consumption. Energy-efficient models help reduce your carbon footprint while keeping your energy bills in check.</span></p><p><br></p><p><span class=\"ql-size-large\">Noise Level</span></p><p><br></p><p><span class=\"ql-size-large\">Consider the noise level produced by the air cooler, especially if you plan to use it in bedrooms or study areas. Look for models that operate quietly to ensure a peaceful environment.</span></p><p><br></p><p><span class=\"ql-size-large\">Portability</span></p><p><br></p><p><span class=\"ql-size-large\">If you require the flexibility to move the air cooler between different rooms, consider its portability features. Look for lightweight models with caster wheels or handles for easy mobility.</span></p><h2><br></h2><h2><span class=\"ql-size-large\">Popular Air Cooler Brands in Nepal</span></h2><p><br></p><p><span class=\"ql-size-large\">Several brands offer high-quality air coolers in Nepal. Stouts have a less sweet flavor than porters and frequently have a bitter coffee flavor from the addition of unmalted roasted barley to the wort. They have a big, creamy head that gives them away. One of the most well-known stouts in the world is perhaps Ireland's Guinness.</span></p><p class=\"ql-align-justify\"><br></p><p class=\"ql-align-justify\"><br></p><h3 class=\"ql-align-justify\"><span class=\"ql-size-large\" style=\"background-color: transparent; color: rgb(67, 67, 67);\">5.             "description": "<h1><span style=\"color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent;\" class=\"ql-size-large\">Brandy Price in Nepal</span></h1><p class=\"ql-align-justify\"><br></p><p class=\"ql-align-justify\"><span class=\"ql-size-large\" style=\"color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">Brandy</span><span class=\"ql-size-large\" style=\"color: rgb(32, 32, 32); background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">&nbsp;is a liquor </span><span class=\"ql-size-large\" style=\"color: rgb(32, 32, 32); background-color: transparent;\">produced</span><span class=\"ql-size-large\" style=\"color: rgb(32, 32, 32); background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\"> by fermented wine. Brandy </span><span class=\"ql-size-large\" style=\"color: rgb(32, 32, 32); background-color: transparent;\">generally</span><span class=\"ql-size-large\" style=\"color: rgb(32, 32, 32); background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\"> contains 35 – 60% alcohol with 80 to 100 proof. Grapes are used to making traditional brandy. The alcohol contains in brandy varies depending on its type.</span></p><p><br></p><p><span class=\"ql-size-large\" style=\"color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent;\"><img src=\"https://lh6.googleusercontent.com/v8ndaIP4Nn-Prtj-pCDNbFokFbBFAGkkJx7BcmxNZ6pvsBJM-joYxsabqL5p42iziUYr4ykUaNGDuLx7nmayV0zgkLX6haDlCuubQV1x5G1M8nKQSzRw6oVhoKoavr8fmOinuULDo8l6DG325JYSLB0WNf3BUlcsZ1Ih_6AsdQSx_GzYtbJnpKDl_u2fgA\" height=\"468\" width=\"624\"></span></p><p><br></p><p><br></p><p class=\"ql-align-justify\"><strong class=\"ql-size-large\" style=\"color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent;\">Brandy price in Nepal</strong><span class=\"ql-size-large\" style=\"color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent;\"> range (small to large) starts at Rs.800/- and goes up to Rs.42,000/- (Approx).</span><span class=\"ql-size-large\" style=\"color: rgb(32, 32, 32); background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\"> Other fruits fall into two-order pome brandy from apples and pears, while gravestones fruit brandies use apricots, cherries, peaches, and gems.</span></p><p class=\"ql-align-justify\"><br></p><p class=\"ql-align-justify\"><br></p><h2><span class=\"ql-size-large\" style=\"color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent;\">Types of Brandy</span></h2><p><br></p><p class=\"ql-align-justify\"><span class=\"ql-size-large\" style=\"color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent;\">So let's introduce you to the various varieties of brandy in order to throw some light on the topic of the alcoholic spirit.</span></p><p class=\"ql-align-justify\"><br></p><h3><span class=\"ql-size-large\" style=\"color: rgb(67, 67, 67); background-color: transparent;\">1. French Brandy</span></h3><p class=\"ql-align-justify\"><br></p><p class=\"ql-align-justify\"><span class=\"ql-size-large\" style=\"color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent;\">Each region of France has its unique microclimate and distinct variations in the soil's composition. This has caused some substantially diverse varieties of brandy to be produced over the years.</span></p><p class=\"ql-align-justify\"><br></p><h4><span class=\"ql-size-large\" style=\"color: rgb(102, 102, 102); background-color: transparent;\">Cognac Brandy</span></h4><p><br></p><p class=\"ql-align-justify\"><span class=\"ql-size-large\" style=\"color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent;\">Cognac, the world's most well-known brandy, can only be produced using grapes produced in the 79,000-hectare AOC region of South West France. Not only that, but brandy must go through a difficult production procedure and be distilled twice in copper pot stills in order to legally use the term \"Cognac.\"&nbsp;</span></p><p><br></p><h4 class=\"ql-align-justify\"><span class=\"ql-size-large\" style=\"color: rgb(102, 102, 102); background-color: transparent;\">Armagnac Brandy</span></h4><p><br></p><p class=\"ql-align-justify\"><span class=\"ql-size-large\" style=\"color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent;\">Similar to Cognac, which comes from South West France and extends into the Pyrenees Mountain foothills, Armagnac is a grape brandy. Similar to Cognac, Armagnac is a grape brandy with AOC certification. The age statements for this brandy are the same as those for Cognac, VS, VSOP, XO, and Hors d'Age. Armagnac and Cognac differ greatly in that Armagnac only goes through one distillation procedure.</span></p><p><br></p><h4><span class=\"ql-size-large\" style=\"color: rgb(102, 102, 102); background-color: transparent;\">Calvados</span></h4><p><br></p><p class=\"ql-align-justify\"><span class=\"ql-size-large\" style=\"color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent;\">Calvados, an apple spirit, can be produced further north in the Normandy region. This area of the world is relatively wet, making it the ideal place to cultivate the small, very flavorful apples used to make the liquor. Calvados is aged in wood and can be either double- or single-distilled.</span></p><p><br></p><h3><span class=\"ql-size-large\" style=\"color: rgb(67, 67, 67); background-color: transparent;\">2. Spanish Brandy</span></h3><p><br></p><p class=\"ql-align-justify\"><span class=\"ql-size-large\" style=\"color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent;\">Grapes are used to making Spanish brandy.&nbsp;In the Andalucian region of Jerez, 95 percent of the production occurs. The remainder is manufactured in Penedes, a region of Catalonia.</span></p><p><br></p><h4 class=\"ql-align-justify\"><span class=\"ql-size-large\" style=\"color: rgb(102, 102, 102); background-color: transparent;\">Brandy de Jerez</span></h4><p><br></p><p class=\"ql-align-justify\"><span class=\"ql-size-large\" style=\"color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent;\">Brandy must be aged in solera-style casks that have previously held sherry in order to be considered a Brandy de Jerez. The \"sherry triangle,\" which is formed by the villages of Sanlucar de Barrameda, El Puerto de Santa Maria, and Jerez de la Frontera, is also where they must mature. Brandy de Jerez is available in three varieties: Solera, Solera Reserva, and Solera Gran Reserva.</span></p><p><br></p><h3><span class=\"ql-size-large\" style=\"color: rgb(67, 67, 67); background-color: transparent;\">3. Obstler Brandy</span></h3><p><br></p><p class=\"ql-align-justify\"><span class=\"ql-size-large\" style=\"color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent;\">Obstler is a fruit brand made in Austria, Switzerland, and Southern Germany's Alpine regions. Fruits like apricots, plums, cherries, apples, pears, or wild berries are used to make it. Schnaps is the name given to it by locals, who describe it as a clear liquid in general. Prior to beginning the maturing process in oak barrels, Obstler is typically double distilled and shares many characteristics with eau-de-vie, the main ingredient in Cognac.</span></p><p><br></p><h3><span class=\"ql-size-large\" style=\"color: rgb(67, 67, 67); background-color: transparent;\">4. Pisco Brandy</span></h3><p><br></p><p class=\"ql-align-justify\"><span class=\"ql-size-large\" style=\"color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent;\">Pisco, a brandy from Chile and Peru, is becoming more and more well-liked. This is particularly true in the US, which, after Chile, imports the most tequila. Despite the fact that Pisco is a brandy derived from grape wine, however, it differs greatly from Cognac and Armagnac. The Pisco Sour cocktail is becoming more and more well-known worldwide.&nbsp;</span></p><p><br></p><h3 class=\"ql-align-justify\"><span class=\"ql-size-large\" style=\"color: rgb(67, 67, 67); background-color: transparent;\">5. Pomace Brandy</span></h3><p class=\"ql-align-justify\"><br></p><p class=\"ql-align-justify\"><span class=\"ql-size-large\" style=\"color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent;\">Brandy known as grappa (Pomace )is produced in San Marino, the Italian section of Switzerland, or Italy. Pomace, or the skin, pulp, seeds, and stems left over from making wine, is used to make it. Anywhere in the world can produce pomace brandy, but only Italian pomace brandy can be called grappa.</span></p><p class=\"ql-align-justify\"><br></p><h2><span class=\"ql-size-large\" style=\"color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent;\">How to buy brandy in Nepal?</span></h2><p><br></p><p class=\"ql-align-justify\"><span class=\"ql-size-large\" style=\"color: rgb(0, 0, 0); background-color: transparent;\">We have a great solution for you all. Acer Predator</span></h3><p class=\"ql-align-justify\"><br></p><p class=\"ql-align-justify\"><span class=\"ql-size-large\" style=\"background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); color: rgb(0, 0, 0);\">For serious gamers, there is the Acer Predator. These laptops come with at least one GeForce GTX 1050 visual card from NVIDIA. You may play video games on high settings this way. You may direct your character in the appropriate direction at all times by using the indicated WASD keys. Furthermore, the Predators include a mix of an SSD and HDD that guarantees quick startup times and enough storage capacity for all of your games.</span></p><p><br></p><p class=\"ql-align-justify\"><strong class=\"ql-size-large\" style=\"background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); color: rgb(17, 17, 17);\">The pros of the Acer Predator:</strong></p><ol><li data-list=\"bullet\" class=\"ql-align-justify\"><span class=\"ql-ui\" contenteditable=\"false\"></span><span class=\"ql-size-large\" style=\"color: rgb(17, 17, 17); background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">Gaming on at least high settings</span></li><li data-list=\"bullet\" class=\"ql-align-justify\"><span class=\"ql-ui\" contenteditable=\"false\"></span><span class=\"ql-size-large\" style=\"color: rgb(17, 17, 17); background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">Equipped with SSD and HDD</span></li><li data-list=\"bullet\" class=\"ql-align-justify\"><span class=\"ql-ui\" contenteditable=\"false\"></span><span class=\"ql-size-large\" style=\"color: rgb(17, 17, 17); background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">Cooler boost for better cooling</span></li></ol><p><br></p><h3><br></h3><h3><span class=\"ql-size-large\" style=\"background-color: transparent; color: rgb(67, 67, 67);\">5. Acer Travelmate</span></h3><p class=\"ql-align-justify\"><br></p><p class=\"ql-align-justify\"><span class=\"ql-size-large\" style=\"background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); color: rgb(17, 17, 17);\">The target market for Acer Travelmate is business users.
